Subject: Call for papers: Monastic Journeys from Late Antiquity to the Middle Ages

Please take note (and disseminate as appropriate) of the enclosed call for papers for a conference on 'Monastic Journeys', the third in a series of events organized by several French academic institutions.

It will be hosted at the Division of Byzantine Research (Institute for Medieval Research, Austrian Academy of Sciences) in Vienna, 17 to 19 November 2016.

With kind regards,

Claudia Rapp
